5624:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
5625:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
5626:    try {
5627:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
5628:        return reply.send({
5629:          period: 'demo',
5630:          total_revenue: 0,
5631:          total_orders: 0,
5632:          average_order_value: 0,
5633:          top_products: [],
5634:          sales_trend: []
5635:        });
5636:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
5637:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
5638:      let pi = 2;
5639:      switch (period) {
5640:        case 'last_7_days':
5641:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
5642:          break;
5643:        case 'last_30_days':
5644:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
5645:          break;
5646:        case 'last_90_days':
5647:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
5648:          break;
5649:        case 'custom':
5650:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
5651:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
5652: + pi;
5653:          params.push(start_date);
5654:          pi++;
5655:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
5656: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
5657:          break;
5658:        default:
5659:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
5660:      }
5661:      const totalQuery = `
5662:        SELECT
5663:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
5664:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
5665:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
5666:        FROM sales_reports sr
5667:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
5668:      `;
5669:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
5670:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
5671:        pool.query(`
5672:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
5673:          FROM sales_reports sr
5674:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
5675:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
5676:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
5677:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
5678:          LIMIT 10
5679:        `, params),
5680:        pool.query(`
5681:          SELECT
5682:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
5683:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
5684:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
5685:          FROM sales_reports sr
5686:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
5687:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
5688:          ORDER BY date ASC
5689:        `, params)
5690:      ]);
5691:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
5692:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
5693:      return reply.send({
5694:        period,
5695:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
5696:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
5697:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
5698:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
5699:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
5700:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
5701:          product_name: r.name,
5702:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
5703:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
5704:        })),
5705:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
5706:          date: r.date,
5707:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
5708:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
5709:        }))
5710:      });
5711:    } catch (err) {
5712:      fastify.log.error(err);
5713:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
5714:    }
5715:  });

5966:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);

6102:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
6103:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
6104:    try {
6105:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
6106:        return reply.send({
6107:          period: 'demo',
6108:          total_revenue: 0,
6109:          total_orders: 0,
6110:          average_order_value: 0,
6111:          top_products: [],
6112:          sales_trend: []
6113:        });
6114:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
6115:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
6116:      let pi = 2;
6117:      switch (period) {
6118:        case 'last_7_days':
6119:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
6120:          break;
6121:        case 'last_30_days':
6122:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
6123:          break;
6124:        case 'last_90_days':
6125:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
6126:          break;
6127:        case 'custom':
6128:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
6129:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
6130: + pi;
6131:          params.push(start_date);
6132:          pi++;
6133:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
6134: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
6135:          break;
6136:        default:
6137:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
6138:      }
6139:      const totalQuery = `
6140:        SELECT
6141:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
6142:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
6143:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
6144:        FROM sales_reports sr
6145:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
6146:      `;
6147:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
6148:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
6149:        pool.query(`
6150:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
6151:          FROM sales_reports sr
6152:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
6153:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
6154:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
6155:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
6156:          LIMIT 10
6157:        `, params),
6158:        pool.query(`
6159:          SELECT
6160:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
6161:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
6162:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
6163:          FROM sales_reports sr
6164:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
6165:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
6166:          ORDER BY date ASC
6167:        `, params)
6168:      ]);
6169:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
6170:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
6171:      return reply.send({
6172:        period,
6173:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
6174:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
6175:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
6176:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
6177:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
6178:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
6179:          product_name: r.name,
6180:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
6181:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
6182:        })),
6183:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
6184:          date: r.date,
6185:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
6186:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
6187:        }))
6188:      });
6189:    } catch (err) {
6190:      fastify.log.error(err);
6191:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
6192:    }
6193:  });

6584:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
6585:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
6586:    try {
6587:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
6588:        return reply.send({
6589:          period: 'demo',
6590:          total_revenue: 0,
6591:          total_orders: 0,
6592:          average_order_value: 0,
6593:          top_products: [],
6594:          sales_trend: []
6595:        });
6596:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
6597:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
6598:      let pi = 2;
6599:      switch (period) {
6600:        case 'last_7_days':
6601:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
6602:          break;
6603:        case 'last_30_days':
6604:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
6605:          break;
6606:        case 'last_90_days':
6607:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
6608:          break;
6609:        case 'custom':
6610:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
6611:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
6612: + pi;
6613:          params.push(start_date);
6614:          pi++;
6615:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
6616: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
6617:          break;
6618:        default:
6619:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
6620:      }
6621:      const totalQuery = `
6622:        SELECT
6623:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
6624:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
6625:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
6626:        FROM sales_reports sr
6627:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
6628:      `;
6629:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
6630:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
6631:        pool.query(`
6632:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
6633:          FROM sales_reports sr
6634:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
6635:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
6636:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
6637:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
6638:          LIMIT 10
6639:        `, params),
6640:        pool.query(`
6641:          SELECT
6642:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
6643:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
6644:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
6645:          FROM sales_reports sr
6646:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
6647:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
6648:          ORDER BY date ASC
6649:        `, params)
6650:      ]);
6651:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
6652:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
6653:      return reply.send({
6654:        period,
6655:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
6656:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
6657:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
6658:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
6659:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
6660:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
6661:          product_name: r.name,
6662:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
6663:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
6664:        })),
6665:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
6666:          date: r.date,
6667:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
6668:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
6669:        }))
6670:      });
6671:    } catch (err) {
6672:      fastify.log.error(err);
6673:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
6674:    }
6675:  });

6893:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
6894:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
6895:      return reply.send({
6896:        period,
6897:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
6898:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
6899:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
6900:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
6901:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
6902:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
6903:          product_name: r.name,
6904:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
6905:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
6906:        })),
6907:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
6908:          date: r.date,
6909:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
6910:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
6911:        }))
6912:      });
6913:    } catch (err) {

6925:        try {
6926:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
6927:        } catch (_) {
6928:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
6929:        }
6930:      }
6931:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';

6934:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
6935:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';

6941:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
6942:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));

7064:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
7065:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
7066:    try {
7067:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
7068:        return reply.send({
7069:          period: 'demo',
7070:          total_revenue: 0,
7071:          total_orders: 0,
7072:          average_order_value: 0,
7073:          top_products: [],
7074:          sales_trend: []
7075:        });
7076:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
7077:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
7078:      let pi = 2;
7079:      switch (period) {
7080:        case 'last_7_days':
7081:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
7082:          break;
7083:        case 'last_30_days':
7084:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
7085:          break;
7086:        case 'last_90_days':
7087:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
7088:          break;
7089:        case 'custom':
7090:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
7091:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
7092: + pi;
7093:          params.push(start_date);
7094:          pi++;
7095:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
7096: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
7097:          break;
7098:        default:
7099:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
7100:      }
7101:      const totalQuery = `
7102:        SELECT
7103:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
7104:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
7105:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
7106:        FROM sales_reports sr
7107:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7108:      `;
7109:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
7110:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
7111:        pool.query(`
7112:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
7113:          FROM sales_reports sr
7114:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
7115:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7116:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
7117:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
7118:          LIMIT 10
7119:        `, params),
7120:        pool.query(`
7121:          SELECT
7122:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
7123:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
7124:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
7125:          FROM sales_reports sr
7126:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7127:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
7128:          ORDER BY date ASC
7129:        `, params)
7130:      ]);
7131:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
7132:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
7133:      return reply.send({
7134:        period,
7135:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
7136:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
7137:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
7138:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
7139:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
7140:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
7141:          product_name: r.name,
7142:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
7143:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
7144:        })),
7145:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
7146:          date: r.date,
7147:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
7148:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
7149:        }))
7150:      });
7151:    } catch (err) {
7152:      fastify.log.error(err);
7153:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
7154:    }
7155:  });

7354:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
7355:          FROM sales_reports sr
7356:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
7357:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7358:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
7359:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
7360:          LIMIT 10
7361:        `, params),
7362:        pool.query(`
7363:          SELECT
7364:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
7365:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
7366:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
7367:          FROM sales_reports sr
7368:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7369:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
7370:          ORDER BY date ASC
7371:        `, params)
7372:      ]);
7373:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
7374:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
7375:      return reply.send({
7376:        period,
7377:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
7378:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
7379:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
7380:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
7381:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
7382:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
7383:          product_name: r.name,
7384:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
7385:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
7386:        })),
7387:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
7388:          date: r.date,
7389:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
7390:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
7391:        }))
7392:      });
7393:    } catch (err) {
7394:      fastify.log.error(err);
7395:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
7396:    }
7397:  });

7400:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
7401:    try {
7402:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
7403:      let ids = [];
7404:      if (product_ids) {
7405:        try {
7406:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
7407:        } catch (_) {
7408:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
7409:        }
7410:      }
7411:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
7412:      let params = [];
7413:      if (ids.length > 0) {
7414:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
7415:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
7416:        params = ids;
7417:      } else {
7418:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
7419:        params = [request.vendorId];
7420:      }
7421:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
7422:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
7423:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
7424:    } catch (err) {
7425:      fastify.log.error(err);
7426:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });

7546:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
7547:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
7548:    try {
7549:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
7550:        return reply.send({
7551:          period: 'demo',
7552:          total_revenue: 0,
7553:          total_orders: 0,
7554:          average_order_value: 0,
7555:          top_products: [],
7556:          sales_trend: []
7557:        });
7558:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
7559:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
7560:      let pi = 2;
7561:      switch (period) {
7562:        case 'last_7_days':
7563:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
7564:          break;
7565:        case 'last_30_days':
7566:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
7567:          break;
7568:        case 'last_90_days':
7569:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
7570:          break;
7571:        case 'custom':
7572:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
7573:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
7574: + pi;
7575:          params.push(start_date);
7576:          pi++;
7577:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
7578: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
7579:          break;
7580:        default:
7581:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
7582:      }
7583:      const totalQuery = `
7584:        SELECT
7585:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
7586:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
7587:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
7588:        FROM sales_reports sr
7589:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7590:      `;
7591:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
7592:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
7593:        pool.query(`
7594:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
7595:          FROM sales_reports sr
7596:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
7597:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7598:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
7599:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
7600:          LIMIT 10
7601:        `, params),
7602:        pool.query(`
7603:          SELECT
7604:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
7605:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
7606:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
7607:          FROM sales_reports sr
7608:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7609:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
7610:          ORDER BY date ASC
7611:        `, params)
7612:      ]);
7613:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
7614:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
7615:      return reply.send({
7616:        period,
7617:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
7618:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
7619:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
7620:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
7621:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
7622:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
7623:          product_name: r.name,
7624:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
7625:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
7626:        })),
7627:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
7628:          date: r.date,
7629:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
7630:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
7631:        }))
7632:      });
7633:    } catch (err) {
7634:      fastify.log.error(err);
7635:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
7636:    }

7817:          params.push(start_date);
7818:          pi++;
7819:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
7820: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
7821:          break;
7822:        default:
7823:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
7824:      }
7825:      const totalQuery = `
7826:        SELECT
7827:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
7828:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
7829:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
7830:        FROM sales_reports sr
7831:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7832:      `;
7833:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
7834:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
7835:        pool.query(`
7836:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
7837:          FROM sales_reports sr
7838:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
7839:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7840:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
7841:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
7842:          LIMIT 10
7843:        `, params),
7844:        pool.query(`
7845:          SELECT
7846:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
7847:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
7848:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
7849:          FROM sales_reports sr
7850:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
7851:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
7852:          ORDER BY date ASC
7853:        `, params)
7854:      ]);
7855:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
7856:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
7857:      return reply.send({
7858:        period,
7859:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
7860:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
7861:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
7862:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
7863:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
7864:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
7865:          product_name: r.name,
7866:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
7867:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
7868:        })),
7869:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
7870:          date: r.date,
7871:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
7872:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
7873:        }))
7874:      });
7875:    } catch (err) {
7876:      fastify.log.error(err);
7877:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
7878:    }
7879:  });

8226:        case 'last_7_days':
8227:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';

8229:        case 'last_30_days':
8230:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
8231:          break;
8232:        case 'last_90_days':
8233:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
8234:          break;
8235:        case 'custom':
8236:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
8237:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
8238: + pi;
8239:          params.push(start_date);
8240:          pi++;
8241:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <=

8246:      }

8249:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
8250:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
8251:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
8252:        FROM sales_reports sr
8253:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8254:      `;

8256:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
8257:        pool.query(`
8258:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
8259:          FROM sales_reports sr
8260:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
8261:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8262:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
8263:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
8264:          LIMIT 10
8265:        `, params),
8266:        pool.query(`
8267:          SELECT
8268:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
8269:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
8270:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
8271:          FROM sales_reports sr
8272:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8273:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
8274:          ORDER BY date ASC
8275:        `, params)
8276:      ]);
8277:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
8278:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;

8450:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
8451:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
8452:    try {
8453:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
8454:        return reply.send({
8455:          period: 'demo',
8456:          total_revenue: 0,
8457:          total_orders: 0,
8458:          average_order_value: 0,
8459:          top_products: [],
8460:          sales_trend: []
8461:        });
8462:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
8463:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
8464:      let pi = 2;
8465:      switch (period) {
8466:        case 'last_7_days':
8467:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
8468:          break;
8469:        case 'last_30_days':
8470:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
8471:          break;
8472:        case 'last_90_days':
8473:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
8474:          break;
8475:        case 'custom':
8476:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
8477:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
8478: + pi;
8479:          params.push(start_date);
8480:          pi++;
8481:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
8482: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
8483:          break;
8484:        default:
8485:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
8486:      }
8487:      const totalQuery = `
8488:        SELECT
8489:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
8490:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
8491:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
8492:        FROM sales_reports sr
8493:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8494:      `;
8495:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
8496:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
8497:        pool.query(`
8498:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
8499:          FROM sales_reports sr
8500:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
8501:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8502:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
8503:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
8504:          LIMIT 10
8505:        `, params),
8506:        pool.query(`
8507:          SELECT
8508:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
8509:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
8510:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
8511:          FROM sales_reports sr
8512:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8513:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
8514:          ORDER BY date ASC
8515:        `, params)
8516:      ]);
8517:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
8518:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
8519:      return reply.send({
8520:        period,
8521:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
8522:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
8523:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
8524:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
8525:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
8526:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
8527:          product_name: r.name,
8528:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
8529:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
8530:        })),
8531:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
8532:          date: r.date,
8533:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
8534:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
8535:        }))
8536:      });
8537:    } catch (err) {
8538:      fastify.log.error(err);
8539:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
8540:    }
8541:  });

8751:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
8752:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
8753:          FROM sales_reports sr
8754:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8755:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
8756:          ORDER BY date ASC
8757:        `, params)
8758:      ]);
8759:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
8760:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
8761:      return reply.send({
8762:        period,
8763:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
8764:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
8765:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
8766:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
8767:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
8768:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
8769:          product_name: r.name,
8770:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
8771:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
8772:        })),
8773:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
8774:          date: r.date,
8775:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
8776:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
8777:        }))
8778:      });
8779:    } catch (err) {
8780:      fastify.log.error(err);
8781:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
8782:    }

8791:        try {
8792:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
8793:        } catch (_) {
8794:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
8795:        }
8796:      }

8800:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '

8804:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
8805:        params = [request.vendorId];
8806:      }
8807:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
8808:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));

8930:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
8931:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
8932:    try {
8933:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
8934:        return reply.send({
8935:          period: 'demo',
8936:          total_revenue: 0,
8937:          total_orders: 0,
8938:          average_order_value: 0,
8939:          top_products: [],
8940:          sales_trend: []
8941:        });
8942:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
8943:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
8944:      let pi = 2;
8945:      switch (period) {
8946:        case 'last_7_days':
8947:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
8948:          break;
8949:        case 'last_30_days':
8950:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
8951:          break;
8952:        case 'last_90_days':
8953:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
8954:          break;
8955:        case 'custom':
8956:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
8957:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
8958: + pi;
8959:          params.push(start_date);
8960:          pi++;
8961:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
8962: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
8963:          break;
8964:        default:
8965:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
8966:      }
8967:      const totalQuery = `
8968:        SELECT
8969:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
8970:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
8971:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
8972:        FROM sales_reports sr
8973:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8974:      `;
8975:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
8976:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
8977:        pool.query(`
8978:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
8979:          FROM sales_reports sr
8980:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
8981:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8982:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
8983:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
8984:          LIMIT 10
8985:        `, params),
8986:        pool.query(`
8987:          SELECT
8988:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
8989:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
8990:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
8991:          FROM sales_reports sr
8992:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
8993:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
8994:          ORDER BY date ASC
8995:        `, params)
8996:      ]);
8997:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
8998:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
8999:      return reply.send({
9000:        period,
9001:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
9002:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
9003:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
9004:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
9005:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
9006:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
9007:          product_name: r.name,
9008:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
9009:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
9010:        })),
9011:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
9012:          date: r.date,
9013:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
9014:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
9015:        }))
9016:      });
9017:    } catch (err) {
9018:      fastify.log.error(err);
9019:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
9020:    }
9021:  });

9214:        FROM sales_reports sr
9215:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9216:      `;
9217:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
9218:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
9219:        pool.query(`
9220:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
9221:          FROM sales_reports sr
9222:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
9223:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9224:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
9225:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
9226:          LIMIT 10
9227:        `, params),
9228:        pool.query(`
9229:          SELECT
9230:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
9231:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
9232:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
9233:          FROM sales_reports sr
9234:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9235:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
9236:          ORDER BY date ASC
9237:        `, params)
9238:      ]);
9239:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
9240:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
9241:      return reply.send({
9242:        period,
9243:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
9244:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
9245:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
9246:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
9247:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),

9249:          product_name: r.name,
9250:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
9251:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
9252:        })),
9253:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
9254:          date: r.date,
9255:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
9256:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
9257:        }))
9258:      });
9259:    } catch (err) {

9426:      let pi = 2;
9427:      switch (period) {
9428:        case 'last_7_days':
9429:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
9430:          break;
9431:        case 'last_30_days':
9432:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
9433:          break;
9434:        case 'last_90_days':
9435:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
9436:          break;
9437:        case 'custom':
9438:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
9439:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
9440: + pi;
9441:          params.push(start_date);
9442:          pi++;
9443:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
9444: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
9445:          break;
9446:        default:
9447:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
9448:      }
9449:      const totalQuery = `
9450:        SELECT
9451:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
9452:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
9453:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
9454:        FROM sales_reports sr
9455:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9456:      `;

9458:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),

9461:          FROM sales_reports sr
9462:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
9463:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9464:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
9465:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
9466:          LIMIT 10
9467:        `, params),

9469:          SELECT
9470:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
9471:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
9472:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
9473:          FROM sales_reports sr
9474:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9475:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
9476:          ORDER BY date ASC
9477:        `, params)
9478:      ]);
9479:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
9480:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
9481:      return reply.send({
9482:        period,

9677:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
9678:          break;
9679:        case 'custom':
9680:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
9681:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
9682: + pi;
9683:          params.push(start_date);
9684:          pi++;
9685:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
9686: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
9687:          break;
9688:        default:
9689:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
9690:      }
9691:      const totalQuery = `
9692:        SELECT
9693:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
9694:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
9695:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
9696:        FROM sales_reports sr
9697:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9698:      `;
9699:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
9700:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
9701:        pool.query(`
9702:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
9703:          FROM sales_reports sr
9704:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
9705:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9706:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
9707:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
9708:          LIMIT 10
9709:        `, params),
9710:        pool.query(`
9711:          SELECT
9712:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
9713:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
9714:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
9715:          FROM sales_reports sr
9716:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
9717:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
9718:          ORDER BY date ASC
9719:        `, params)
9720:      ]);
9721:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
9722:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
9723:      return reply.send({
9724:        period,
9725:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
9726:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
9727:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
9728:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
9729:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
9730:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
9731:          product_name: r.name,
9732:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
9733:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
9734:        })),
9735:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
9736:          date: r.date,
9737:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
9738:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
9739:        }))
9740:      });
9741:    } catch (err) {
9742:      fastify.log.error(err);
9743:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
9744:    }

9747:  // ── GET /vendor/products/ai-flags ────────────────────────────────────────────
9748:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
9749:    try {
9750:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
9751:      let ids = [];
9752:      if (product_ids) {
9753:        try {
9754:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
9755:        } catch (_) {
9756:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
9757:        }
9758:      }
9759:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
9760:      let params = [];
9761:      if (ids.length > 0) {
9762:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
9763:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
9764:        params = ids;
9765:      } else {
9766:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
9767:        params = [request.vendorId];
9768:      }
9769:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
9770:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
9771:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
9772:    } catch (err) {
9773:      fastify.log.error(err);
9774:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
9775:    }
9776:  });

10144:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
10145:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
10146:      let pi = 2;
10147:      switch (period) {
10148:        case 'last_7_days':
10149:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
10150:          break;
10151:        case 'last_30_days':
10152:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
10153:          break;
10154:        case 'last_90_days':
10155:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
10156:          break;
10157:        case 'custom':
10158:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
10159:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
10160: + pi;
10161:          params.push(start_date);
10162:          pi++;
10163:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
10164: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
10165:          break;
10166:        default:
10167:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
10168:      }
10169:      const totalQuery = `
10170:        SELECT
10171:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
10172:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
10173:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
10174:        FROM sales_reports sr
10175:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
10176:      `;
10177:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
10178:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
10179:        pool.query(`
10180:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
10181:          FROM sales_reports sr
10182:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
10183:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
10184:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
10185:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
10186:          LIMIT 10
10187:        `, params),
10188:        pool.query(`
10189:          SELECT
10190:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
10191:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
10192:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
10193:          FROM sales_reports sr
10194:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
10195:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
10196:          ORDER BY date ASC
10197:        `, params)
10198:      ]);
10199:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
10200:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
10201:      return reply.send({
10202:        period,
10203:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
10204:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
10205:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
10206:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
10207:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
10208:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
10209:          product_name: r.name,
10210:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
10211:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
10212:        })),
10213:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
10214:          date: r.date,
10215:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
10216:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
10217:        }))
10218:      });

10607:      return reply.send({ sales_reports: rows, pagination: { currentPage: np, totalPages: Math.ceil(total / nl), totalItems: total, itemsPerPage: nl } });
10608:    } catch (err) {
10609:      fastify.log.error(err);
10610:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch sales reports', code: 'FETCH_SALES_FAILED', details: err.message });
10611:    }

10614:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
10615:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
10616:    try {
10617:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
10618:        return reply.send({
10619:          period: 'demo',
10620:          total_revenue: 0,
10621:          total_orders: 0,
10622:          average_order_value: 0,
10623:          top_products: [],
10624:          sales_trend: []
10625:        });
10626:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
10627:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
10628:      let pi = 2;
10629:      switch (period) {
10630:        case 'last_7_days':
10631:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
10632:          break;
10633:        case 'last_30_days':
10634:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
10635:          break;
10636:        case 'last_90_days':
10637:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
10638:          break;
10639:        case 'custom':
10640:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
10641:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
10642: + pi;
10643:          params.push(start_date);
10644:          pi++;
10645:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
10646: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
10647:          break;
10648:        default:
10649:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
10650:      }
10651:      const totalQuery = `
10652:        SELECT
10653:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
10654:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
10655:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
10656:        FROM sales_reports sr
10657:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
10658:      `;
10659:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
10660:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
10661:        pool.query(`
10662:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
10663:          FROM sales_reports sr
10664:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
10665:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
10666:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
10667:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
10668:          LIMIT 10
10669:        `, params),
10670:        pool.query(`
10671:          SELECT
10672:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
10673:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
10674:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
10675:          FROM sales_reports sr
10676:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
10677:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
10678:          ORDER BY date ASC
10679:        `, params)
10680:      ]);
10681:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
10682:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
10683:      return reply.send({
10684:        period,
10685:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
10686:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
10687:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
10688:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
10689:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
10690:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
10691:          product_name: r.name,
10692:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
10693:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
10694:        })),
10695:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
10696:          date: r.date,
10697:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
10698:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
10699:        }))
10700:      });
10701:    } catch (err) {
10702:      fastify.log.error(err);
10703:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
10704:    }
10705:  });

10709:    try {

10711:      let ids = [];

10713:        try {
10714:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
10715:        } catch (_) {
10716:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
10717:        }
10718:      }
10719:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
10720:      let params = [];

10722:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
10723:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
10724:        params = ids;
10725:      } else {
10726:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
10727:        params = [request.vendorId];
10728:      }
10729:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
10730:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
10731:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
10732:    } catch (err) {

10734:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });

11071:      params.push(nl, offset);
11072:      const qt = `
11073:        SELECT sr.*, p.name as product_name_from_product
11074:        FROM sales_reports sr
11075:        LEFT JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
11076:        ${wc}
11077:        ORDER BY sr.created_at DESC
11078:        LIMIT ${pi} OFFSET ${pi + 1}
11079:      `;
11080:      const result = await pool.query(qt, params);
11081:      const cr = await pool.query('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sales_reports sr ' + wc, params.slice(0, -2));
11082:      const total = parseInt(cr.rows[0].count);
11083:      const rows = result.rows.map(r => ({
11084:        ...r,
11085:        product_name: r.product_name_from_product || r.product_name
11086:      }));
11087:      return reply.send({ sales_reports: rows, pagination: { currentPage: np, totalPages: Math.ceil(total / nl), totalItems: total, itemsPerPage: nl } });
11088:    } catch (err) {
11089:      fastify.log.error(err);
11090:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch sales reports', code: 'FETCH_SALES_FAILED', details: err.message });
11091:    }
11092:  });

11094:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
11095:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
11096:    try {
11097:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
11098:        return reply.send({
11099:          period: 'demo',
11100:          total_revenue: 0,
11101:          total_orders: 0,
11102:          average_order_value: 0,
11103:          top_products: [],
11104:          sales_trend: []
11105:        });
11106:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
11107:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
11108:      let pi = 2;
11109:      switch (period) {
11110:        case 'last_7_days':
11111:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
11112:          break;
11113:        case 'last_30_days':
11114:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
11115:          break;
11116:        case 'last_90_days':
11117:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
11118:          break;
11119:        case 'custom':
11120:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
11121:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
11122: + pi;
11123:          params.push(start_date);
11124:          pi++;
11125:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
11126: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
11127:          break;
11128:        default:
11129:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
11130:      }
11131:      const totalQuery = `
11132:        SELECT
11133:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
11134:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
11135:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
11136:        FROM sales_reports sr
11137:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
11138:      `;
11139:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
11140:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
11141:        pool.query(`
11142:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
11143:          FROM sales_reports sr
11144:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
11145:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
11146:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
11147:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
11148:          LIMIT 10
11149:        `, params),
11150:        pool.query(`
11151:          SELECT
11152:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
11153:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
11154:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
11155:          FROM sales_reports sr
11156:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
11157:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
11158:          ORDER BY date ASC
11159:        `, params)
11160:      ]);
11161:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
11162:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
11163:      return reply.send({
11164:        period,
11165:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
11166:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
11167:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
11168:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
11169:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
11170:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
11171:          product_name: r.name,
11172:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
11173:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
11174:        })),
11175:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
11176:          date: r.date,
11177:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
11178:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
11179:        }))
11180:      });
11181:    } catch (err) {
11182:      fastify.log.error(err);
11183:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
11184:    }
11185:  });

11189:    try {
11190:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
11191:      let ids = [];
11192:      if (product_ids) {
11193:        try {
11194:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
11195:        } catch (_) {
11196:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
11197:        }
11198:      }
11199:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
11200:      let params = [];

11202:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
11203:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
11204:        params = ids;
11205:      } else {
11206:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
11207:        params = [request.vendorId];
11208:      }
11209:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
11210:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
11211:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
11212:    } catch (err) {
11213:      fastify.log.error(err);
11214:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });

11576:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
11577:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
11578:    try {
11579:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
11580:        return reply.send({
11581:          period: 'demo',
11582:          total_revenue: 0,
11583:          total_orders: 0,
11584:          average_order_value: 0,
11585:          top_products: [],
11586:          sales_trend: []
11587:        });
11588:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
11589:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
11590:      let pi = 2;
11591:      switch (period) {
11592:        case 'last_7_days':
11593:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
11594:          break;
11595:        case 'last_30_days':
11596:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
11597:          break;
11598:        case 'last_90_days':
11599:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
11600:          break;
11601:        case 'custom':
11602:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
11603:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
11604: + pi;
11605:          params.push(start_date);
11606:          pi++;
11607:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
11608: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
11609:          break;
11610:        default:
11611:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
11612:      }
11613:      const totalQuery = `
11614:        SELECT
11615:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
11616:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
11617:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
11618:        FROM sales_reports sr
11619:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
11620:      `;
11621:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
11622:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
11623:        pool.query(`
11624:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
11625:          FROM sales_reports sr
11626:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
11627:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
11628:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
11629:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
11630:          LIMIT 10
11631:        `, params),
11632:        pool.query(`
11633:          SELECT
11634:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
11635:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
11636:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
11637:          FROM sales_reports sr
11638:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
11639:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
11640:          ORDER BY date ASC
11641:        `, params)
11642:      ]);
11643:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
11644:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
11645:      return reply.send({
11646:        period,
11647:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
11648:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
11649:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
11650:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
11651:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
11652:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
11653:          product_name: r.name,
11654:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
11655:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
11656:        })),
11657:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
11658:          date: r.date,
11659:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
11660:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
11661:        }))
11662:      });
11663:    } catch (err) {
11664:      fastify.log.error(err);
11665:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
11666:    }
11667:  });

11671:    try {
11672:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
11673:      let ids = [];
11674:      if (product_ids) {
11675:        try {
11676:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
11677:        } catch (_) {
11678:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
11679:        }
11680:      }
11681:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
11682:      let params = [];
11683:      if (ids.length > 0) {
11684:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
11685:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
11686:        params = ids;
11687:      } else {
11688:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
11689:        params = [request.vendorId];
11690:      }
11691:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
11692:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
11693:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
11694:    } catch (err) {

11998:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch sales reports', code: 'FETCH_SALES_FAILED', details: err.message });
11999:    }

12002:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
12003:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
12004:    try {
12005:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
12006:        return reply.send({
12007:          period: 'demo',
12008:          total_revenue: 0,
12009:          total_orders: 0,
12010:          average_order_value: 0,
12011:          top_products: [],
12012:          sales_trend: []
12013:        });
12014:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
12015:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
12016:      let pi = 2;
12017:      switch (period) {
12018:        case 'last_7_days':
12019:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
12020:          break;
12021:        case 'last_30_days':
12022:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
12023:          break;
12024:        case 'last_90_days':
12025:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
12026:          break;
12027:        case 'custom':
12028:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
12029:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
12030: + pi;
12031:          params.push(start_date);
12032:          pi++;
12033:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
12034: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
12035:          break;
12036:        default:
12037:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
12038:      }
12039:      const totalQuery = `
12040:        SELECT
12041:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
12042:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
12043:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
12044:        FROM sales_reports sr
12045:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
12046:      `;
12047:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
12048:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
12049:        pool.query(`
12050:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
12051:          FROM sales_reports sr
12052:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
12053:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
12054:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
12055:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
12056:          LIMIT 10
12057:        `, params),
12058:        pool.query(`
12059:          SELECT
12060:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
12061:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
12062:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
12063:          FROM sales_reports sr
12064:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
12065:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
12066:          ORDER BY date ASC
12067:        `, params)
12068:      ]);
12069:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
12070:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
12071:      return reply.send({
12072:        period,
12073:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
12074:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
12075:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
12076:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
12077:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
12078:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
12079:          product_name: r.name,
12080:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
12081:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
12082:        })),
12083:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
12084:          date: r.date,
12085:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
12086:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
12087:        }))
12088:      });
12089:    } catch (err) {
12090:      fastify.log.error(err);
12091:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
12092:    }
12093:  });

12096:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
12097:    try {
12098:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
12099:      let ids = [];
12100:      if (product_ids) {
12101:        try {
12102:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
12103:        } catch (_) {
12104:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
12105:        }
12106:      }
12107:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
12108:      let params = [];
12109:      if (ids.length > 0) {
12110:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
12111:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
12112:        params = ids;
12113:      } else {
12114:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
12115:        params = [request.vendorId];
12116:      }
12117:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
12118:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
12119:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
12120:    } catch (err) {
12121:      fastify.log.error(err);
12122:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
12123:    }
12124:  });

12464:        FROM sales_reports sr
12465:        LEFT JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
12466:        ${wc}
12467:        ORDER BY sr.created_at DESC
12468:        LIMIT ${pi} OFFSET ${pi + 1}
12469:      `;
12470:      const result = await pool.query(qt, params);
12471:      const cr = await pool.query('SELECT COUNT(*) FROM sales_reports sr ' + wc, params.slice(0, -2));
12472:      const total = parseInt(cr.rows[0].count);
12473:      const rows = result.rows.map(r => ({
12474:        ...r,
12475:        product_name: r.product_name_from_product || r.product_name
12476:      }));
12477:      return reply.send({ sales_reports: rows, pagination: { currentPage: np, totalPages: Math.ceil(total / nl), totalItems: total, itemsPerPage: nl } });
12478:    } catch (err) {
12479:      fastify.log.error(err);
12480:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch sales reports', code: 'FETCH_SALES_FAILED', details: err.message });
12481:    }
12482:  });

12484:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
12485:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
12486:    try {
12487:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
12488:        return reply.send({
12489:          period: 'demo',
12490:          total_revenue: 0,
12491:          total_orders: 0,
12492:          average_order_value: 0,
12493:          top_products: [],
12494:          sales_trend: []
12495:        });
12496:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
12497:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
12498:      let pi = 2;
12499:      switch (period) {
12500:        case 'last_7_days':
12501:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
12502:          break;
12503:        case 'last_30_days':
12504:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
12505:          break;
12506:        case 'last_90_days':
12507:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
12508:          break;
12509:        case 'custom':
12510:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
12511:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
12512: + pi;
12513:          params.push(start_date);
12514:          pi++;
12515:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
12516: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
12517:          break;
12518:        default:
12519:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
12520:      }
12521:      const totalQuery = `
12522:        SELECT
12523:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
12524:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
12525:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
12526:        FROM sales_reports sr
12527:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
12528:      `;
12529:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
12530:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
12531:        pool.query(`
12532:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
12533:          FROM sales_reports sr
12534:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
12535:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
12536:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
12537:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
12538:          LIMIT 10
12539:        `, params),
12540:        pool.query(`
12541:          SELECT
12542:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
12543:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
12544:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
12545:          FROM sales_reports sr
12546:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
12547:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
12548:          ORDER BY date ASC
12549:        `, params)
12550:      ]);
12551:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
12552:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
12553:      return reply.send({
12554:        period,
12555:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
12556:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
12557:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
12558:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
12559:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
12560:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
12561:          product_name: r.name,
12562:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
12563:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
12564:        })),
12565:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
12566:          date: r.date,
12567:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
12568:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
12569:        }))
12570:      });
12571:    } catch (err) {
12572:      fastify.log.error(err);
12573:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
12574:    }
12575:  });

12587:        }
