12964:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
12965:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
12966:    try {
12967:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
12968:        return reply.send({
12969:          period: 'demo',
12970:          total_revenue: 0,
12971:          total_orders: 0,
12972:          average_order_value: 0,
12973:          top_products: [],
12974:          sales_trend: []
12975:        });
12976:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
12977:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
12978:      let pi = 2;
12979:      switch (period) {
12980:        case 'last_7_days':
12981:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
12982:          break;
12983:        case 'last_30_days':
12984:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
12985:          break;
12986:        case 'last_90_days':
12987:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
12988:          break;
12989:        case 'custom':
12990:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
12991:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
12992: + pi;
12993:          params.push(start_date);
12994:          pi++;
12995:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
12996: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
12997:          break;
12998:        default:
12999:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
13000:      }
13001:      const totalQuery = `
13002:        SELECT
13003:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
13004:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
13005:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
13006:        FROM sales_reports sr
13007:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13008:      `;
13009:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
13010:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
13011:        pool.query(`
13012:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
13013:          FROM sales_reports sr
13014:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
13015:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13016:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
13017:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
13018:          LIMIT 10
13019:        `, params),
13020:        pool.query(`
13021:          SELECT
13022:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
13023:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
13024:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
13025:          FROM sales_reports sr
13026:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13027:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
13028:          ORDER BY date ASC
13029:        `, params)
13030:      ]);
13031:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
13032:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
13033:      return reply.send({
13034:        period,
13035:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
13036:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
13037:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
13038:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
13039:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
13040:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
13041:          product_name: r.name,
13042:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
13043:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
13044:        })),
13045:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
13046:          date: r.date,
13047:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
13048:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
13049:        }))
13050:      });
13051:    } catch (err) {
13052:      fastify.log.error(err);
13053:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
13054:    }
13055:  });

13057:  // ── GET /vendor/products/ai-flags ────────────────────────────────────────────
13058:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
13059:    try {
13060:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
13061:      let ids = [];
13062:      if (product_ids) {
13063:        try {
13064:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
13065:        } catch (_) {
13066:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
13067:        }
13068:      }
13069:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
13070:      let params = [];
13071:      if (ids.length > 0) {
13072:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
13073:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
13074:        params = ids;
13075:      } else {
13076:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
13077:        params = [request.vendorId];
13078:      }
13079:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
13080:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
13081:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
13082:    } catch (err) {
13083:      fastify.log.error(err);
13084:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
13085:    }
13086:  });

13091:      const { id } = request.params;
13092:      const pid = Number(id);
13093:      const pr = await pool.query('SELECT id, vendor_id FROM products WHERE id = $1', [pid]);
13094:      if (pr.rows.length === 0 || pr.rows[0].vendor_id !== request.vendorId)
13095:        return reply.code(404).send({ error: 'Product not found or you do not have permission.', code: 'PRODUCT_NOT_FOUND' });
13096:      let result = await pool.query('SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id = $1', [pid]);
13097:      if (result.rows.length === 0) {
13098:        const analysis = await analyzeProductRisk(pid);
13099:        if (!analysis) return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to analyze product risk', code: 'ANALYSIS_FAILED' });
13100:        result = await pool.query('SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id = $1', [pid]);
13101:      }
13102:      const row = result.rows[0];
13103:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: { risk_score: row.risk_score, flags: row.flags || [], updated_at: row.updated_at } });
13104:    } catch (err) {

13446:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
13447:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
13448:    try {
13449:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
13450:        return reply.send({
13451:          period: 'demo',
13452:          total_revenue: 0,
13453:          total_orders: 0,
13454:          average_order_value: 0,
13455:          top_products: [],
13456:          sales_trend: []
13457:        });
13458:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
13459:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
13460:      let pi = 2;
13461:      switch (period) {
13462:        case 'last_7_days':
13463:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
13464:          break;
13465:        case 'last_30_days':
13466:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
13467:          break;
13468:        case 'last_90_days':
13469:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
13470:          break;
13471:        case 'custom':
13472:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
13473:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
13474: + pi;
13475:          params.push(start_date);
13476:          pi++;
13477:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
13478: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
13479:          break;
13480:        default:
13481:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
13482:      }
13483:      const totalQuery = `
13484:        SELECT
13485:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
13486:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
13487:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
13488:        FROM sales_reports sr
13489:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13490:      `;
13491:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
13492:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
13493:        pool.query(`
13494:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
13495:          FROM sales_reports sr
13496:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
13497:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13498:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
13499:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
13500:          LIMIT 10
13501:        `, params),
13502:        pool.query(`
13503:          SELECT
13504:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
13505:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
13506:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
13507:          FROM sales_reports sr
13508:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13509:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
13510:          ORDER BY date ASC
13511:        `, params)
13512:      ]);
13513:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
13514:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
13515:      return reply.send({
13516:        period,
13517:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
13518:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
13519:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
13520:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
13521:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
13522:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
13523:          product_name: r.name,
13524:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
13525:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
13526:        })),
13527:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
13528:          date: r.date,
13529:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
13530:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
13531:        }))
13532:      });
13533:    } catch (err) {
13534:      fastify.log.error(err);
13535:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
13536:    }
13537:  });

13539:  // ── GET /vendor/products/ai-flags ────────────────────────────────────────────
13540:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
13541:    try {
13542:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
13543:      let ids = [];
13544:      if (product_ids) {
13545:        try {
13546:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
13547:        } catch (_) {
13548:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
13549:        }
13550:      }
13551:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
13552:      let params = [];
13553:      if (ids.length > 0) {
13554:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
13555:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
13556:        params = ids;
13557:      } else {
13558:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
13559:        params = [request.vendorId];
13560:      }
13561:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
13562:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
13563:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
13564:    } catch (err) {
13565:      fastify.log.error(err);
13566:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
13567:    }
13568:  });

13572:    try {
13573:      const { id } = request.params;
13574:      const pid = Number(id);
13575:      const pr = await pool.query('SELECT id, vendor_id FROM products WHERE id = $1', [pid]);
13576:      if (pr.rows.length === 0 || pr.rows[0].vendor_id !== request.vendorId)
13577:        return reply.code(404).send({ error: 'Product not found or you do not have permission.', code: 'PRODUCT_NOT_FOUND' });
13578:      let result = await pool.query('SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id = $1', [pid]);
13579:      if (result.rows.length === 0) {
13580:        const analysis = await analyzeProductRisk(pid);
13581:        if (!analysis) return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to analyze product risk', code: 'ANALYSIS_FAILED' });
13582:        result = await pool.query('SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id = $1', [pid]);
13583:      }
13584:      const row = result.rows[0];
13585:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: { risk_score: row.risk_score, flags: row.flags || [], updated_at: row.updated_at } });
13586:    } catch (err) {
13587:      fastify.log.error(err);
13588:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });

13861:        return reply.code(404).send({ error: 'Product not found or you do not have permission.', code: 'PRODUCT_NOT_FOUND' });

13924:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
13925:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
13926:    try {
13927:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
13928:        return reply.send({
13929:          period: 'demo',
13930:          total_revenue: 0,
13931:          total_orders: 0,
13932:          average_order_value: 0,
13933:          top_products: [],
13934:          sales_trend: []
13935:        });
13936:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
13937:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
13938:      let pi = 2;
13939:      switch (period) {
13940:        case 'last_7_days':
13941:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
13942:          break;
13943:        case 'last_30_days':
13944:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
13945:          break;
13946:        case 'last_90_days':
13947:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
13948:          break;
13949:        case 'custom':
13950:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
13951:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
13952: + pi;
13953:          params.push(start_date);
13954:          pi++;
13955:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
13956: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
13957:          break;
13958:        default:
13959:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
13960:      }
13961:      const totalQuery = `
13962:        SELECT
13963:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
13964:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
13965:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
13966:        FROM sales_reports sr
13967:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13968:      `;
13969:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
13970:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
13971:        pool.query(`
13972:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
13973:          FROM sales_reports sr
13974:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
13975:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13976:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
13977:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
13978:          LIMIT 10
13979:        `, params),
13980:        pool.query(`
13981:          SELECT
13982:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
13983:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
13984:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
13985:          FROM sales_reports sr
13986:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
13987:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
13988:          ORDER BY date ASC
13989:        `, params)
13990:      ]);
13991:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
13992:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
13993:      return reply.send({
13994:        period,
13995:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
13996:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
13997:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
13998:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
13999:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
14000:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
14001:          product_name: r.name,
14002:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
14003:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
14004:        })),
14005:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
14006:          date: r.date,
14007:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
14008:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
14009:        }))
14010:      });
14011:    } catch (err) {
14012:      fastify.log.error(err);
14013:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
14014:    }
14015:  });

14017:  // ── GET /vendor/products/ai-flags ────────────────────────────────────────────
14018:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
14019:    try {
14020:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
14021:      let ids = [];
14022:      if (product_ids) {
14023:        try {
14024:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
14025:        } catch (_) {
14026:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
14027:        }
14028:      }
14029:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
14030:      let params = [];
14031:      if (ids.length > 0) {
14032:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
14033:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
14034:        params = ids;
14035:      } else {
14036:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
14037:        params = [request.vendorId];
14038:      }
14039:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
14040:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
14041:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
14042:    } catch (err) {
14043:      fastify.log.error(err);
14044:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
14045:    }
14046:  });

14406:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
14407:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
14408:    try {
14409:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
14410:        return reply.send({
14411:          period: 'demo',
14412:          total_revenue: 0,
14413:          total_orders: 0,
14414:          average_order_value: 0,
14415:          top_products: [],
14416:          sales_trend: []
14417:        });
14418:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
14419:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
14420:      let pi = 2;
14421:      switch (period) {
14422:        case 'last_7_days':
14423:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
14424:          break;
14425:        case 'last_30_days':
14426:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
14427:          break;
14428:        case 'last_90_days':
14429:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
14430:          break;
14431:        case 'custom':
14432:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
14433:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
14434: + pi;
14435:          params.push(start_date);
14436:          pi++;
14437:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
14438: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
14439:          break;
14440:        default:
14441:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
14442:      }
14443:      const totalQuery = `
14444:        SELECT
14445:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
14446:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
14447:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
14448:        FROM sales_reports sr
14449:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
14450:      `;
14451:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
14452:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
14453:        pool.query(`
14454:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
14455:          FROM sales_reports sr
14456:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
14457:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
14458:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
14459:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
14460:          LIMIT 10
14461:        `, params),
14462:        pool.query(`
14463:          SELECT
14464:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
14465:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
14466:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
14467:          FROM sales_reports sr
14468:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
14469:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
14470:          ORDER BY date ASC
14471:        `, params)
14472:      ]);
14473:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
14474:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
14475:      return reply.send({
14476:        period,
14477:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
14478:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
14479:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
14480:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
14481:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
14482:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
14483:          product_name: r.name,
14484:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
14485:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
14486:        })),
14487:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
14488:          date: r.date,
14489:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
14490:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
14491:        }))
14492:      });
14493:    } catch (err) {
14494:      fastify.log.error(err);
14495:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
14496:    }
14497:  });

14886:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
14887:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
14888:    try {
14889:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
14890:        return reply.send({
14891:          period: 'demo',
14892:          total_revenue: 0,
14893:          total_orders: 0,
14894:          average_order_value: 0,
14895:          top_products: [],
14896:          sales_trend: []
14897:        });
14898:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
14899:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
14900:      let pi = 2;
14901:      switch (period) {
14902:        case 'last_7_days':
14903:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
14904:          break;
14905:        case 'last_30_days':
14906:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
14907:          break;
14908:        case 'last_90_days':
14909:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
14910:          break;
14911:        case 'custom':
14912:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
14913:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
14914: + pi;
14915:          params.push(start_date);
14916:          pi++;
14917:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
14918: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
14919:          break;
14920:        default:
14921:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
14922:      }
14923:      const totalQuery = `
14924:        SELECT
14925:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
14926:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
14927:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
14928:        FROM sales_reports sr
14929:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
14930:      `;
14931:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
14932:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
14933:        pool.query(`
14934:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
14935:          FROM sales_reports sr
14936:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
14937:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
14938:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
14939:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
14940:          LIMIT 10
14941:        `, params),
14942:        pool.query(`
14943:          SELECT
14944:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
14945:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
14946:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
14947:          FROM sales_reports sr
14948:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
14949:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
14950:          ORDER BY date ASC
14951:        `, params)
14952:      ]);
14953:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
14954:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
14955:      return reply.send({
14956:        period,
14957:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
14958:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
14959:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
14960:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
14961:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
14962:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
14963:          product_name: r.name,
14964:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
14965:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
14966:        })),
14967:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
14968:          date: r.date,
14969:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
14970:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
14971:        }))
14972:      });
14973:    } catch (err) {
14974:      fastify.log.error(err);
14975:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
14976:    }
14977:  });

14979:  // ── GET /vendor/products/ai-flags ────────────────────────────────────────────
14980:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
14981:    try {
14982:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
14983:      let ids = [];
14984:      if (product_ids) {
14985:        try {
14986:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
14987:        } catch (_) {
14988:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
14989:        }
14990:      }
14991:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
14992:      let params = [];
14993:      if (ids.length > 0) {
14994:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
14995:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
14996:        params = ids;
14997:      } else {
14998:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
14999:        params = [request.vendorId];
15000:      }
15001:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
15002:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
15003:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
15004:    } catch (err) {
15005:      fastify.log.error(err);
15006:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
15007:    }
15008:  });

15368:  // ── GET /vendor/analytics ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
15369:  fastify.get('/vendor/analytics', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
15370:    try {
15371:      if (!pool.dbConnected)
15372:        return reply.send({
15373:          period: 'demo',
15374:          total_revenue: 0,
15375:          total_orders: 0,
15376:          average_order_value: 0,
15377:          top_products: [],
15378:          sales_trend: []
15379:        });
15380:      const { period = 'last_30_days', start_date, end_date, group_by = 'day' } = request.query;
15381:      let dateCondition, params = [request.vendorId];
15382:      let pi = 2;
15383:      switch (period) {
15384:        case 'last_7_days':
15385:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'7 days\'';
15386:          break;
15387:        case 'last_30_days':
15388:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
15389:          break;
15390:        case 'last_90_days':
15391:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'90 days\'';
15392:          break;
15393:        case 'custom':
15394:          if (!start_date) return reply.code(400).send({ error: 'start_date required for custom period', code: 'MISSING_START_DATE' });
15395:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= 
15396: + pi;
15397:          params.push(start_date);
15398:          pi++;
15399:          if (end_date) { dateCondition += ' AND sr.report_date <= 
15400: + pi; params.push(end_date); pi++; }
15401:          break;
15402:        default:
15403:          dateCondition = 'sr.report_date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL \'30 days\'';
15404:      }
15405:      const totalQuery = `
15406:        SELECT
15407:          COUNT(*) as order_count,
15408:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.quantity), 0) as total_quantity,
15409:          COALESCE(SUM(sr.total_amount), 0) as total_revenue
15410:        FROM sales_reports sr
15411:        WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
15412:      `;
15413:      const [totalRes, topRes, trendRes] = await Promise.all([
15414:        pool.query(totalQuery, params),
15415:        pool.query(`
15416:          SELECT p.name, SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity, SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue
15417:          FROM sales_reports sr
15418:          JOIN products p ON sr.product_id = p.id
15419:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
15420:          GROUP BY p.id, p.name
15421:          ORDER BY revenue DESC
15422:          LIMIT 10
15423:        `, params),
15424:        pool.query(`
15425:          SELECT
15426:            DATE(sr.report_date) as date,
15427:            SUM(sr.total_amount) as revenue,
15428:            SUM(sr.quantity) as quantity
15429:          FROM sales_reports sr
15430:          WHERE sr.vendor_id = $1 AND ${dateCondition}
15431:          GROUP BY DATE(sr.report_date)
15432:          ORDER BY date ASC
15433:        `, params)
15434:      ]);
15435:      const total = totalRes.rows[0];
15436:      const aov = total.order_count > 0 ? total.total_revenue / total.order_count : 0;
15437:      return reply.send({
15438:        period,
15439:        date_range: { start_date, end_date },
15440:        total_revenue: parseFloat(total.total_revenue),
15441:        total_orders: parseInt(total.order_count),
15442:        total_quantity: parseInt(total.quantity),
15443:        average_order_value: parseFloat(aov.toFixed(2)),
15444:        top_products: topRes.rows.map(r => ({
15445:          product_name: r.name,
15446:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity),
15447:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue)
15448:        })),
15449:        sales_trend: trendRes.rows.map(r => ({
15450:          date: r.date,
15451:          revenue: parseFloat(r.revenue),
15452:          quantity: parseInt(r.quantity)
15453:        }))
15454:      });
15455:    } catch (err) {
15456:      fastify.log.error(err);
15457:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch analytics', code: 'FETCH_ANALYTICS_FAILED', details: err.message });
15458:    }
15459:  });

15462:  fastify.get('/vendor/products/ai-flags', { preHandler: auth }, async (request, reply) => {
15463:    try {
15464:      const { product_ids } = request.query;
15465:      let ids = [];
15466:      if (product_ids) {
15467:        try {
15468:          ids = JSON.parse(product_ids);
15469:        } catch (_) {
15470:          ids = product_ids.split(',').map(s => Number(s.trim())).filter(n => Number.isFinite(n));
15471:        }
15472:      }
15473:      let query = 'SELECT product_id, risk_score, flags, updated_at FROM product_ai_flags WHERE product_id IN (';
15474:      let params = [];
15475:      if (ids.length > 0) {
15476:        const ph = ids.map((_, i) => '
15477:        query += ph + ') ORDER BY product_id';
15478:        params = ids;
15479:      } else {
15480:        query += 'SELECT product_id FROM products WHERE vendor_id = $1) ORDER BY product_id';
15481:        params = [request.vendorId];
15482:      }
15483:      const result = await pool.query(query, params);
15484:      const flagsMap = Object.fromEntries(result.rows.map(r => [r.product_id, { risk_score: r.risk_score, flags: r.flags || [], updated_at: r.updated_at }]));
15485:      return reply.send({ ai_flags: flagsMap, count: result.rows.length });
15486:    } catch (err) {
15487:      fastify.log.error(err);
15488:      return reply.code(500).send({ error: 'Unable to fetch AI flags', code: 'FETCH_AI_FLAGS_FAILED' });
